import requests import json import os from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("Searching for book information with DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") # First, try to resolve the DOI directly doi_url = "https://doi.org/10.1353/book.24372" headers = { "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36" } try: print(f"Attempting to resolve DOI URL: {doi_url}") response = requests.get(doi_url, headers=headers, allow_redirects=True) print(f"Response status code: {response.status_code}") print(f"Final URL after redirection: {response.url}") # Save the redirected page content for analysis with open('workspace/doi_page.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print("Saved DOI page content to workspace/doi_page.html") # Parse the HTML using BeautifulSoup soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Try to extract title title = soup.find('title') if title: print(f"Page title: {title.text.strip()}") # Look for structured metadata meta_tags = soup.find_all('meta') print("\nExtracting metadata:") metadata = {} for tag in meta_tags: if tag.get('name') and tag.get('content'): metadata[tag['name']] = tag['content'] if tag['name'] in ['citation_title', 'dc.title', 'og:title', 'title']: print(f"Title from metadata: {tag['content']}") elif tag['name'] in ['citation_author', 'dc.creator', 'author']: print(f"Author from metadata: {tag['content']}") # Save metadata for reference with open('workspace/metadata.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(metadata, f, indent=2) print("Saved metadata to workspace/metadata.json") # Try to extract main content main_content = soup.find('main') or soup.find('article') or soup.find('div', class_=re.compile(r'(content|main|article)')) if main_content: print("\nExtracting main content preview:") text_content = main_content.get_text(separator='\n', strip=True) preview = text_content[:500] + '...' if len(text_content) > 500 else text_content print(preview) with open('workspace/main_content.txt', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(text_content) print("Saved main content to workspace/main_content.txt") # Look for download links or access options download_links = [] for link in soup.find_all('a', href=True): href = link['href'].lower() text = link.get_text().lower() if any(term in href or term in text for term in ['pdf', 'download', 'full text', 'read', 'chapter', 'access']): download_links.append({ 'text': link.get_text().strip(), 'url': link['href'] }) if download_links: print("\nPotential download/access links:") for i, link in enumerate(download_links[:10], 1): print(f"{i}. {link['text']} - {link['url']}") if len(download_links) > 10: print(f"... and {len(download_links) - 10} more links") else: print("\nNo obvious download/access links found") # Try to specifically identify chapter 2 chapter_links = [] for link in soup.find_all('a', href=True): text = link.get_text().lower() if 'chapter 2' in text or (('chapter' in text or 'ch' in text) and '2' in text): chapter_links.append({ 'text': link.get_text().strip(), 'url': link['href'] }) if chapter_links: print("\nPotential Chapter 2 links:") for i, link in enumerate(chapter_links, 1): print(f"{i}. {link['text']} - {link['url']}") # Look for any mentions of neurologist names text_content = soup.get_text() neurologist_patterns = [r'(?:Dr\.|Professor|neurologist)\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', r'([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)(?:\s+was|\s+is|,\s+the\s+neurologist)'] print("\nSearching for neurologist mentions:") for pattern in neurologist_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, text_content) if matches: print(f"Potential neurologist names: {', '.join(set(matches))}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error resolving DOI: {e}") # If the DOI resolution doesn't provide enough information, try CrossRef API print("\nQuerying CrossRef API for additional DOI information...") try: crossref_url = f"https://api.crossref.org/works/10.1353/book.24372" response = requests.get(crossref_url, headers=headers) print(f"CrossRef API response status code: {response.status_code}") if response.status_code == 200: crossref_data = response.json() with open('workspace/crossref_data.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(crossref_data, f, indent=2) print("Saved CrossRef data to workspace/crossref_data.json") if 'message' in crossref_data: message = crossref_data['message'] if 'title' in message and message['title']: print(f"\nBook title from CrossRef: {message['title'][0]}") if 'author' in message and message['author']: authors = [] for author in message['author']: if 'given' in author and 'family' in author: authors.append(f"{author['given']} {author['family']}") elif 'name' in author: authors.append(author['name']) if authors: print(f"Authors from CrossRef: {', '.join(authors)}") if 'publisher' in message: print(f"Publisher: {message['publisher']}") if 'published' in message: print(f"Published: {message['published']['date-parts'][0][0]}") else: print(f"CrossRef API error: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error querying CrossRef API: {e}") # Try Google Books API for additional information print("\nQuerying Google Books API for related information...") try: # Search for books by title or DOI information we've gathered so far search_term = "10.1353/book.24372" if 'metadata' in locals() and metadata.get('citation_title'): search_term = metadata['citation_title'] elif 'crossref_data' in locals() and 'message' in crossref_data and 'title' in crossref_data['message']: search_term = crossref_data['message']['title'][0] google_books_url = f"https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes?q={search_term}" response = requests.get(google_books_url) print(f"Google Books API response status code: {response.status_code}") if response.status_code == 200: books_data = response.json() with open('workspace/google_books_data.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(books_data, f, indent=2) print("Saved Google Books data to workspace/google_books_data.json") if 'items' in books_data and books_data['items']: book = books_data['items'][0]['volumeInfo'] # Take the first result print("\nBook information from Google Books:") if 'title' in book: print(f"Title: {book['title']}") if 'subtitle' in book: print(f"Subtitle: {book['subtitle']}") if 'authors' in book: print(f"Authors: {', '.join(book['authors'])}") if 'description' in book: desc = book['description'] print(f"Description: {desc[:300]}..." if len(desc) > 300 else f"Description: {desc}") if 'infoLink' in book: print(f"More info: {book['infoLink']}") # Look for neurologist name in description if 'description' in book: matches = re.findall(r'(?:neurologist|doctor|Dr\.|physician)\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', book['description']) if matches: print(f"\nPotential neurologist mentioned: {', '.join(set(matches))}") # Check for mentions of "endopsychic myths" or related terms if 'description' in book: if re.search(r'endopsychic\s+myths?', book['description'], re.IGNORECASE): print("\nFound mention of 'endopsychic myths' in book description") context = re.search(r'([^.]*endopsychic\s+myths?[^.]*\.)', book['description'], re.IGNORECASE) if context: print(f"Context: {context.group(1)}") else: print(f"Google Books API error: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error querying Google Books API: {e}") # Use Project MUSE to try to find the book print("\nSearching Project MUSE for DOI 10.1353/book.24372...") try: # Project MUSE often hosts books with the 10.1353 prefix muse_url = "https://muse.jhu.edu/search?action=search&query=doi:10.1353/book.24372" response = requests.get(muse_url, headers=headers) print(f"Project MUSE search response status code: {response.status_code}") # Save the response for analysis with open('workspace/muse_search_results.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print("Saved Project MUSE search results to workspace/muse_search_results.html") # Parse the HTML soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') search_results = soup.find_all('div', class_='result') if search_results: print(f"Found {len(search_results)} results on Project MUSE") for i, result in enumerate(search_results[:3], 1): title_element = result.find('h1') or result.find('h2') or result.find('h3') title = title_element.text.strip() if title_element else "Title not found" author_element = result.find('div', class_='authors') or result.find('div', class_='author') author = author_element.text.strip() if author_element else "Author not found" link_element = result.find('a') link = link_element['href'] if link_element and 'href' in link_element.attrs else "Link not found" print(f"\nResult {i}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Author: {author}") print(f"Link: {link}") # Follow the first result to get more details if i == 1 and link and link.startswith('/'): full_link = "https://muse.jhu.edu" + link print(f"\nFollowing link to get more details: {full_link}") detail_response = requests.get(full_link, headers=headers) if detail_response.status_code == 200: with open('workspace/muse_book_details.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(detail_response.text) print("Saved book details to workspace/muse_book_details.html") # Parse details page detail_soup = BeautifulSoup(detail_response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for chapter list or table of contents toc_element = detail_soup.find('div', class_=re.compile(r'toc|table-of-contents')) if toc_element: print("\nFound Table of Contents:") chapters = toc_element.find_all('li') or toc_element.find_all('div', class_='chapter') for chapter in chapters[:10]: # Show first 10 chapters print(f"- {chapter.get_text().strip()}") # Look specifically for Chapter 2 if re.search(r'chapter\s+2|2\.\s', chapter.get_text().lower()): chapter_link = chapter.find('a') if chapter_link and 'href' in chapter_link.attrs: ch_url = chapter_link['href'] if not ch_url.startswith('http'): ch_url = "https://muse.jhu.edu" + ch_url print(f"\nFound Chapter 2 link: {ch_url}") # Look for book summary or abstract abstract = detail_soup.find('div', class_=re.compile(r'abstract|summary|description')) if abstract: print("\nBook Summary:") print(abstract.get_text().strip()) # Check for neurologist mentions text = abstract.get_text() matches = re.findall(r'(?:neurologist|doctor|Dr\.)\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', text) if matches: print(f"\nPotential neurologist mentioned: {', '.join(set(matches))}") else: print("No direct results found on Project MUSE") except Exception as e: print(f"Error searching Project MUSE: {e}") print("\nSearch completed. Summary of findings:") print("-------------------------------------------") print("All extracted data has been saved to files in the workspace directory.") print("Please review the output files for complete information.")

import requests import json import os from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("Searching for book information with DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") # First, try to resolve the DOI directly doi_url = "https://doi.org/10.1353/book.24372" headers = { "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36" } try: print(f"Attempting to resolve DOI URL: {doi_url}") response = requests.get(doi_url, headers=headers, allow_redirects=True) print(f"Response status code: {response.status_code}") print(f"Final URL after redirection: {response.url}") # Save the redirected page content for analysis with open('workspace/doi_page.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print("Saved DOI page content to workspace/doi_page.html") # Parse the HTML using BeautifulSoup soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Try to extract title title = soup.find('title') if title: print(f"Page title: {title.text.strip()}") # Look for structured metadata meta_tags = soup.find_all('meta') print("\nExtracting metadata:") metadata = {} for tag in meta_tags: if tag.get('name') and tag.get('content'): metadata[tag['name']] = tag['content'] if tag['name'] in ['citation_title', 'dc.title', 'og:title', 'title']: print(f"Title from metadata: {tag['content']}") elif tag['name'] in ['citation_author', 'dc.creator', 'author']: print(f"Author from metadata: {tag['content']}") # Save metadata for reference with open('workspace/metadata.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(metadata, f, indent=2) print("Saved metadata to workspace/metadata.json") # Try to extract main content main_content = soup.find('main') or soup.find('article') or soup.find('div', class_=re.compile(r'(content|main|article)')) if main_content: print("\nExtracting main content preview:") text_content = main_content.get_text(separator='\n', strip=True) preview = text_content[:500] + '...' if len(text_content) > 500 else text_content print(preview) with open('workspace/main_content.txt', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(text_content) print("Saved main content to workspace/main_content.txt") # Look for download links or access options download_links = [] for link in soup.find_all('a', href=True): href = link['href'].lower() text = link.get_text().lower() if any(term in href or term in text for term in ['pdf', 'download', 'full text', 'read', 'chapter', 'access']): download_links.append({ 'text': link.get_text().strip(), 'url': link['href'] }) if download_links: print("\nPotential download/access links:") for i, link in enumerate(download_links[:10], 1): print(f"{i}. {link['text']} - {link['url']}") if len(download_links) > 10: print(f"... and {len(download_links) - 10} more links") else: print("\nNo obvious download/access links found") # Try to specifically identify chapter 2 chapter_links = [] for link in soup.find_all('a', href=True): text = link.get_text().lower() if 'chapter 2' in text or (('chapter' in text or 'ch' in text) and '2' in text): chapter_links.append({ 'text': link.get_text().strip(), 'url': link['href'] }) if chapter_links: print("\nPotential Chapter 2 links:") for i, link in enumerate(chapter_links, 1): print(f"{i}. {link['text']} - {link['url']}") # Look for any mentions of neurologist names text_content = soup.get_text() neurologist_patterns = [r'(?:Dr\.|Professor|neurologist)\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', r'([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)(?:\s+was|\s+is|,\s+the\s+neurologist)'] print("\nSearching for neurologist mentions:") for pattern in neurologist_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, text_content) if matches: print(f"Potential neurologist names: {', '.join(set(matches))}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error resolving DOI: {e}") # If the DOI resolution doesn't provide enough information, try CrossRef API print("\nQuerying CrossRef API for additional DOI information...") try: crossref_url = f"https://api.crossref.org/works/10.1353/book.24372" response = requests.get(crossref_url, headers=headers) print(f"CrossRef API response status code: {response.status_code}") if response.status_code == 200: crossref_data = response.json() with open('workspace/crossref_data.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(crossref_data, f, indent=2) print("Saved CrossRef data to workspace/crossref_data.json") if 'message' in crossref_data: message = crossref_data['message'] if 'title' in message and message['title']: print(f"\nBook title from CrossRef: {message['title'][0]}") if 'author' in message and message['author']: authors = [] for author in message['author']: if 'given' in author and 'family' in author: authors.append(f"{author['given']} {author['family']}") elif 'name' in author: authors.append(author['name']) if authors: print(f"Authors from CrossRef: {', '.join(authors)}") if 'publisher' in message: print(f"Publisher: {message['publisher']}") if 'published' in message: print(f"Published: {message['published']['date-parts'][0][0]}") else: print(f"CrossRef API error: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error querying CrossRef API: {e}") # Try Google Books API for additional information print("\nQuerying Google Books API for related information...") try: # Search for books by title or DOI information we've gathered so far search_term = "10.1353/book.24372" if 'metadata' in locals() and metadata.get('citation_title'): search_term = metadata['citation_title'] elif 'crossref_data' in locals() and 'message' in crossref_data and 'title' in crossref_data['message']: search_term = crossref_data['message']['title'][0] google_books_url = f"https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes?q={search_term}" response = requests.get(google_books_url) print(f"Google Books API response status code: {response.status_code}") if response.status_code == 200: books_data = response.json() with open('workspace/google_books_data.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(books_data, f, indent=2) print("Saved Google Books data to workspace/google_books_data.json") if 'items' in books_data and books_data['items']: book = books_data['items'][0]['volumeInfo'] # Take the first result print("\nBook information from Google Books:") if 'title' in book: print(f"Title: {book['title']}") if 'subtitle' in book: print(f"Subtitle: {book['subtitle']}") if 'authors' in book: print(f"Authors: {', '.join(book['authors'])}") if 'description' in book: desc = book['description'] print(f"Description: {desc[:300]}..." if len(desc) > 300 else f"Description: {desc}") if 'infoLink' in book: print(f"More info: {book['infoLink']}") # Look for neurologist name in description if 'description' in book: matches = re.findall(r'(?:neurologist|doctor|Dr\.|physician)\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', book['description']) if matches: print(f"\nPotential neurologist mentioned: {', '.join(set(matches))}") # Check for mentions of "endopsychic myths" or related terms if 'description' in book: if re.search(r'endopsychic\s+myths?', book['description'], re.IGNORECASE): print("\nFound mention of 'endopsychic myths' in book description") context = re.search(r'([^.]*endopsychic\s+myths?[^.]*\.)', book['description'], re.IGNORECASE) if context: print(f"Context: {context.group(1)}") else: print(f"Google Books API error: {response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error querying Google Books API: {e}") # Use Project MUSE to try to find the book print("\nSearching Project MUSE for DOI 10.1353/book.24372...") try: # Project MUSE often hosts books with the 10.1353 prefix muse_url = "https://muse.jhu.edu/search?action=search&query=doi:10.1353/book.24372" response = requests.get(muse_url, headers=headers) print(f"Project MUSE search response status code: {response.status_code}") # Save the response for analysis with open('workspace/muse_search_results.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print("Saved Project MUSE search results to workspace/muse_search_results.html") # Parse the HTML soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') search_results = soup.find_all('div', class_='result') if search_results: print(f"Found {len(search_results)} results on Project MUSE") for i, result in enumerate(search_results[:3], 1): title_element = result.find('h1') or result.find('h2') or result.find('h3') title = title_element.text.strip() if title_element else "Title not found" author_element = result.find('div', class_='authors') or result.find('div', class_='author') author = author_element.text.strip() if author_element else "Author not found" link_element = result.find('a') link = link_element['href'] if link_element and 'href' in link_element.attrs else "Link not found" print(f"\nResult {i}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Author: {author}") print(f"Link: {link}") # Follow the first result to get more details if i == 1 and link and link.startswith('/'): full_link = "https://muse.jhu.edu" + link print(f"\nFollowing link to get more details: {full_link}") detail_response = requests.get(full_link, headers=headers) if detail_response.status_code == 200: with open('workspace/muse_book_details.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(detail_response.text) print("Saved book details to workspace/muse_book_details.html") # Parse details page detail_soup = BeautifulSoup(detail_response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for chapter list or table of contents toc_element = detail_soup.find('div', class_=re.compile(r'toc|table-of-contents')) if toc_element: print("\nFound Table of Contents:") chapters = toc_element.find_all('li') or toc_element.find_all('div', class_='chapter') for chapter in chapters[:10]: # Show first 10 chapters print(f"- {chapter.get_text().strip()}") # Look specifically for Chapter 2 if re.search(r'chapter\s+2|2\.\s', chapter.get_text().lower()): chapter_link = chapter.find('a') if chapter_link and 'href' in chapter_link.attrs: ch_url = chapter_link['href'] if not ch_url.startswith('http'): ch_url = "https://muse.jhu.edu" + ch_url print(f"\nFound Chapter 2 link: {ch_url}") # Look for book summary or abstract abstract = detail_soup.find('div', class_=re.compile(r'abstract|summary|description')) if abstract: print("\nBook Summary:") print(abstract.get_text().strip()) # Check for neurologist mentions text = abstract.get_text() matches = re.findall(r'(?:neurologist|doctor|Dr\.)\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', text) if matches: print(f"\nPotential neurologist mentioned: {', '.join(set(matches))}") else: print("No direct results found on Project MUSE") except Exception as e: print(f"Error searching Project MUSE: {e}") print("\nSearch completed. Summary of findings:") print("-------------------------------------------") print("All extracted data has been saved to files in the workspace directory.") print("Please review the output files for complete information.")

import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("Analyzing saved data files and performing deeper search for chapter 2 information") # First, examine the workspace directory workspace_files = os.listdir('workspace') print(f"Files in workspace: {workspace_files}") # Analyze the CrossRef data which should have more detailed book information if 'crossref_data.json' in workspace_files: print("\nExamining CrossRef data for book details...") with open('workspace/crossref_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: crossref_data = json.load(f) # Print the structure to understand what we're working with print("CrossRef data structure:") if 'message' in crossref_data: message = crossref_data['message'] print(f"Message keys: {list(message.keys())}") # Extract and print basic book information book_title = message.get('title', ["Unknown"])[0] if 'title' in message else "Unknown" print(f"\nBook Title: {book_title}") # Get ISBN if available if 'ISBN' in message: print(f"ISBN: {', '.join(message['ISBN'])}") # Get DOI doi = message.get('DOI', 'Unknown') print(f"DOI: {doi}") # Get publisher publisher = message.get('publisher', 'Unknown') print(f"Publisher: {publisher}") # Get any URLs provided by CrossRef if 'link' in message: print("\nCrossRef provided links:") for link in message['link']: print(f"- {link.get('URL', 'No URL')} ({link.get('content-type', 'Unknown type')})") # Analyze Google Books data which may have more content details if 'google_books_data.json' in workspace_files: print("\nExamining Google Books data for detailed content...") with open('workspace/google_books_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: books_data = json.load(f) if 'items' in books_data and books_data['items']: # Get first book result book_info = books_data['items'][0]['volumeInfo'] print(f"Google Books Title: {book_info.get('title', 'Unknown')}") if 'subtitle' in book_info: print(f"Subtitle: {book_info.get('subtitle', '')}") if 'authors' in book_info: print(f"Authors: {', '.join(book_info.get('authors', []))}") # Get full description which might mention the neurologist and endopsychic myths if 'description' in book_info: description = book_info['description'] print(f"\nFull Description:\n{description}") # Look for mentions of neurologists with more comprehensive patterns neuro_patterns = [ r'neurologist\s+([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)', r'([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)\s+(?:was|is)\s+a\s+neurologist', r'Dr\.?\s+([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)', r'([A-Z][a-z]+)\s+(?:was|is)\s+(?:a|the)\s+(?:famous|notable|well-known)?\s*neurologist', # Names that appear near neurological terms r'(?:brain|neurology|neurological)\s+(?:[^.]{0,50})\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', # Look for specific neurologists who might be associated with Freud r'(?:Karl Abraham|Alfred Adler|Lou Andreas-Salomé|August Aichhorn|Ludwig Binswanger|Josef Breuer|Helene Deutsch|Paul Federn|Otto Fenichel|Sándor Ferenczi|Anna Freud|Ernest Jones|Carl Jung|Melanie Klein|Karl König|Theodor Reik|Wilhelm Reich)' ] print("\nSearching for neurologist references in description:") for pattern in neuro_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if matches: print(f"Found potential neurologist mentions: {', '.join(set(matches))}") # Look for endopsychic myths mentions print("\nSearching for 'endopsychic myths' references:") endo_patterns = [ r'([^.]*endopsychic\s+myths?[^.]*\.)', r'([^.]*myths?\s+of\s+the\s+unconscious[^.]*\.)', r'([^.]*psychoanalytic\s+myths?[^.]*\.)', r'([^.]*myths?\s+in\s+psychoanalysis[^.]*\.)' ] for pattern in endo_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if matches: print(f"Found related myth concepts: {matches}") # Get industry identifiers like ISBN if 'industryIdentifiers' in book_info: print("\nIndustry Identifiers:") for identifier in book_info['industryIdentifiers']: print(f"{identifier.get('type', 'Unknown')}: {identifier.get('identifier', 'Unknown')}") # Check if there's a preview available if 'previewLink' in book_info: preview_link = book_info['previewLink'] print(f"\nGoogle Books Preview Link: {preview_link}") print("Attempting to access preview to look for chapter 2 information...") try: preview_response = requests.get(preview_link, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"}) if preview_response.status_code == 200: preview_soup = BeautifulSoup(preview_response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for table of contents toc_elements = preview_soup.find_all(['div', 'span', 'p'], string=re.compile(r'Contents|Table of Contents', re.IGNORECASE)) if toc_elements: print("Found potential table of contents in preview") for elem in toc_elements: parent = elem.parent content = parent.get_text(strip=True) print(f"TOC element: {content[:100]}...") # Look specifically for chapter 2 chapter_two = re.search(r'(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+(?:2|II|Two)\s*[:.\-–—]\s*([^\n.]+)', content, re.IGNORECASE) if chapter_two: print(f"\nChapter 2 title may be: {chapter_two.group(1)}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing preview: {e}") # import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("Analyzing saved data files and performing deeper search for chapter 2 information") # First, examine the workspace directory workspace_files = os.listdir('workspace') print(f"Files in workspace: {workspace_files}") # Analyze the CrossRef data which should have more detailed book information if 'crossref_data.json' in workspace_files: print("\nExamining CrossRef data for book details...") with open('workspace/crossref_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: crossref_data = json.load(f) # Print the structure to understand what we're working with print("CrossRef data structure:") if 'message' in crossref_data: message = crossref_data['message'] print(f"Message keys: {list(message.keys())}") # Extract and print basic book information book_title = message.get('title', ["Unknown"])[0] if 'title' in message else "Unknown" print(f"\nBook Title: {book_title}") # Get ISBN if available if 'ISBN' in message: print(f"ISBN: {', '.join(message['ISBN'])}") # Get DOI doi = message.get('DOI', 'Unknown') print(f"DOI: {doi}") # Get publisher publisher = message.get('publisher', 'Unknown') print(f"Publisher: {publisher}") # Get any URLs provided by CrossRef if 'link' in message: print("\nCrossRef provided links:") for link in message['link']: print(f"- {link.get('URL', 'No URL')} ({link.get('content-type', 'Unknown type')})") # Analyze Google Books data which may have more content details if 'google_books_data.json' in workspace_files: print("\nExamining Google Books data for detailed content...") with open('workspace/google_books_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: books_data = json.load(f) if 'items' in books_data and books_data['items']: # Get first book result book_info = books_data['items'][0]['volumeInfo'] print(f"Google Books Title: {book_info.get('title', 'Unknown')}") if 'subtitle' in book_info: print(f"Subtitle: {book_info.get('subtitle', '')}") if 'authors' in book_info: print(f"Authors: {', '.join(book_info.get('authors', []))}") # Get full description which might mention the neurologist and endopsychic myths if 'description' in book_info: description = book_info['description'] print(f"\nFull Description:\n{description}") # Look for mentions of neurologists with more comprehensive patterns neuro_patterns = [ r'neurologist\s+([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)', r'([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)\s+(?:was|is)\s+a\s+neurologist', r'Dr\.?\s+([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)', r'([A-Z][a-z]+)\s+(?:was|is)\s+(?:a|the)\s+(?:famous|notable|well-known)?\s*neurologist', # Names that appear near neurological terms r'(?:brain|neurology|neurological)\s+(?:[^.]{0,50})\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)', # Look for specific neurologists who might be associated with Freud r'(?:Karl Abraham|Alfred Adler|Lou Andreas-Salomé|August Aichhorn|Ludwig Binswanger|Josef Breuer|Helene Deutsch|Paul Federn|Otto Fenichel|Sándor Ferenczi|Anna Freud|Ernest Jones|Carl Jung|Melanie Klein|Karl König|Theodor Reik|Wilhelm Reich)' ] print("\nSearching for neurologist references in description:") for pattern in neuro_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if matches: print(f"Found potential neurologist mentions: {', '.join(set(matches))}") # Look for endopsychic myths mentions print("\nSearching for 'endopsychic myths' references:") endo_patterns = [ r'([^.]*endopsychic\s+myths?[^.]*\.)', r'([^.]*myths?\s+of\s+the\s+unconscious[^.]*\.)', r'([^.]*psychoanalytic\s+myths?[^.]*\.)', r'([^.]*myths?\s+in\s+psychoanalysis[^.]*\.)' ] for pattern in endo_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if matches: print(f"Found related myth concepts: {matches}") # Get industry identifiers like ISBN if 'industryIdentifiers' in book_info: print("\nIndustry Identifiers:") for identifier in book_info['industryIdentifiers']: print(f"{identifier.get('type', 'Unknown')}: {identifier.get('identifier', 'Unknown')}") # Check if there's a preview available if 'previewLink' in book_info: preview_link = book_info['previewLink'] print(f"\nGoogle Books Preview Link: {preview_link}") print("Attempting to access preview to look for chapter 2 information...") try: preview_response = requests.get(preview_link, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"}) if preview_response.status_code == 200: preview_soup = BeautifulSoup(preview_response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for table of contents toc_elements = preview_soup.find_all(['div', 'span', 'p'], string=re.compile(r'Contents|Table of Contents', re.IGNORECASE)) if toc_elements: print("Found potential table of contents in preview") for elem in toc_elements: parent = elem.parent content = parent.get_text(strip=True) print(f"TOC element: {content[:100]}...") # Look specifically for chapter 2 chapter_two = re.search(r'(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+(?:2|II|Two)\s*[:.\-–—]\s*([^\n.]+)', content, re.IGNORECASE) if chapter_two: print(f"\nChapter 2 title may be: {chapter_two.group(1)}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing preview: {e}") # Try to access the full text using the DOI through Unpaywall or Open Access sources print("\nAttempting to locate full text through alternative sources...") doi = "10.1353/book.24372" # Try Unpaywall API try: unpaywall_url = f"https://api.unpaywall.org/v2/{doi}?email=researcher@example.com" print(f"Querying Unpaywall API: {unpaywall_url}") unpaywall_response = requests.get(unpaywall_url) if unpaywall_response.status_code == 200: unpaywall_data = unpaywall_response.json() print(f"Unpaywall response received, status: {unpaywall_data.get('is_oa', False)}") # Save Unpaywall data with open('workspace/unpaywall_data.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(unpaywall_data, f, indent=2) # Check for open access links if unpaywall_data.get('is_oa', False): print("This publication is Open Access!") if 'best_oa_location' in unpaywall_data and unpaywall_data['best_oa_location']: oa_url = unpaywall_data['best_oa_location'].get('url') if oa_url: print(f"Best OA URL: {oa_url}") print("Attempting to access full text...") try: oa_response = requests.get(oa_url, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"}) if oa_response.status_code == 200: with open('workspace/fulltext.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(oa_response.text) print("Full text saved to workspace/fulltext.html") # Parse for chapter information oa_soup = BeautifulSoup(oa_response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for chapter 2 chapter_headers = oa_soup.find_all(['h1', 'h2', 'h3', 'h4'], string=re.compile(r'Chapter\s+2|Chapter\s+II', re.IGNORECASE)) if chapter_headers: print("\nFound Chapter 2 in full text!") for header in chapter_headers: print(f"Chapter title: {header.get_text(strip=True)}") # Try to get the content following this header chapter_content = "" next_elem = header.find_next() while next_elem and next_elem.name not in ['h1', 'h2', 'h3', 'h4']: if next_elem.name == 'p': chapter_content += next_elem.get_text() + "\n\n" next_elem = next_elem.find_next() # Print a preview and save to file preview = chapter_content[:500] + "..." if len(chapter_content) > 500 else chapter_content print(f"Chapter 2 preview:\n{preview}") with open('workspace/chapter2_content.txt', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(chapter_content) print("Chapter 2 content saved to workspace/chapter2_content.txt") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing OA URL: {e}") else: print("This publication is not available as Open Access through Unpaywall.") else: print(f"Unpaywall API error: {unpaywall_response.status_code} - {unpaywall_response.text}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error querying Unpaywall: {e}") # Try to find more information about the book using its title and ISBN print("\nSearching for additional book information using title and any ISBN...") # Get book title and ISBN from our previous searches book_title = "" book_isbn = "" if 'google_books_data.json' in workspace_files: with open('workspace/google_books_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: books_data = json.load(f) if 'items' in books_data and books_data['items']: book_info = books_data['items'][0]['volumeInfo'] book_title = book_info.get('title', '') if 'subtitle' in book_info: book_title += ": " + book_info.get('subtitle', '') if 'industryIdentifiers' in book_info: for identifier in book_info['industryIdentifiers']: if identifier.get('type') in ['ISBN_10', 'ISBN_13']: book_isbn = identifier.get('identifier', '') break # Search for more specific information using the book title + "chapter 2" + "endopsychic myths" if book_title: search_query = f"{book_title} chapter 2 endopsychic myths" print(f"Searching for: {search_query}") # Simulate a Google search - this would normally use a proper API google_url = "https://www.google.com/search" headers = { "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36" } params = {"q": search_query} try: search_response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, params=params) if search_response.status_code == 200: # import os import json import requests import re from bs4 import BeautifulSoup print("Continuing investigation of book DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") print("Looking for neurologist information and chapter 2 content on endopsychic myths") print("-" * 80) # First, let's analyze what we know so far print("SUMMARY OF FINDINGS SO FAR:") print("Book Title: A Dark Trace: Sigmund Freud on the Sense of Guilt") print("Author: Herman Westerink") print("Publisher: Leuven University Press (2009)") print("DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") print("ISBN: 9789058677549 / 9058677540") print("Series: Figures of the Unconscious, No. 8") print() print("Key mentions: Carl Jung and Melanie Klein appear as psychoanalysts") print("Freud himself was a neurologist before developing psychoanalysis") print("-" * 80) # Check if we need to update our search approach print("UPDATING SEARCH APPROACH:") print("1. We need to determine if Freud is the neurologist in question") print("2. Find specific information about chapter 2 and endopsychic myths") print("3. Identify the author who influenced beliefs about endopsychic myths") print() # Define search parameters search_queries = [ "A Dark Trace Sigmund Freud Westerink chapter 2", "A Dark Trace Sigmund Freud endopsychic myths", "Sigmund Freud endopsychic myths influence", "Freud neurologist endopsychic myths author influence" ] # List of file paths to check workspace_dir = "workspace" files_to_check = [ "doi_page.html", "metadata.json", "crossref_data.json", "google_books_data.json", "muse_search_results.html" ] # Verify files exist and output their size for file in files_to_check: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.exists(file_path): size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f"File {file} exists ({size} bytes)") else: print(f"File {file} not found") print() # Function to extract text content from HTML safely def extract_text(html_content): soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.extract() # Get text text = soup.get_text(separator="\n", strip=True) return text # Load Google Books data for deeper analysis print("ANALYZING GOOGLE BOOKS DATA FOR CHAPTER INFORMATION:") try: with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, "google_books_data.json"), "r", encoding="utf-8") as f: google_data = json.load(f) # Get volume info if 'items' in google_data and len(google_data['items']) > 0: volume_info = google_data['items'][0]['volumeInfo'] # Check if we can access the book content access_info = google_data['items'][0].get('accessInfo', {}) viewability = access_info.get('viewability', 'NO_PAGES') print(f"Google Books viewability: {viewability}") # Get preview link preview_link = volume_info.get('previewLink') if preview_link: print(f"Preview link: {preview_link}") # Try to access the preview print("Attempting to access book preview...") headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} response = requests.get(preview_link, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save preview page preview_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, "google_preview.html") with open(preview_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Preview page saved to {preview_file}") # Look for table of contents or chapter information preview_text = extract_text(response.text) toc_match = re.search(r"(?:TABLE OF CONTENTS|Contents)[\s\S]*?(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s*[\d]|(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+[\d][^\n]*", preview_text) if toc_match: print("\nFound table of contents or chapter information:") print(toc_match.group(0)) # Look specifically for chapter 2 chapter2_match = re.search(r"(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+(?:2|II|Two)[^\n]*", preview_text) if chapter2_match: print("\nFound Chapter 2 reference:") print(chapter2_match.group(0)) # Look for any content about endopsychic myths endopsychic_match = re.search(r"[^\n.]*endopsychic[^\n.]*", preview_text) if endopsychic_match: print("\nFound endopsychic reference:") print(endopsychic_match.group(0)) else: print("No preview link available") # Check for industry identifiers and other metadata industry_ids = volume_info.get('industryIdentifiers', []) for id_info in industry_ids: print(f"{id_info.get('type')}: {id_info.get('identifier')}") # Check categories or subject categories = volume_info.get('categories', []) if categories: print(f"\nBook categories: {', '.join(categories)}") # Check for other useful information if 'description' in volume_info: # Extract sentences mentioning specific topics description = volume_info['description'] # Look for sentences mentioning neurologists or specific people persons_of_interest = ['Freud', 'Jung', 'Klein', 'Breuer', 'Fliess'] for person in persons_of_interest: matches = re.findall(f"[^.]*\b{person}\b[^.]*\.", description) for match in matches: print(f"\nReference to {person}: {match.strip()}") else: print("No items found in Google Books data") except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing Google Books data: {e}") # We need to determine if Freud is the neurologist in question") print("2. Find specific information about chapter 2 and endopsychic myths") print("3. Identify the author who influenced beliefs about endopsychic myths") print() # Define search parameters search_queries = [ "A Dark Trace Sigmund Freud Westerink chapter 2", "A Dark Trace Sigmund Freud endopsychic myths", "Sigmund Freud endopsychic myths influence", "Freud neurologist endopsychic myths author influence" ] # List of file paths to check workspace_dir = "workspace" files_to_check = [ "doi_page.html", "metadata.json", "crossref_data.json", "google_books_data.json", "muse_search_results.html" ] # Verify files exist and output their size for file in files_to_check: file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file) if os.path.exists(file_path): size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f"File {file} exists ({size} bytes)") else: print(f"File {file} not found") print() # Function to extract text content from HTML safely def extract_text(html_content): soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.extract() # Get text text = soup.get_text(separator="\n", strip=True) return text # Load Google Books data for deeper analysis print("ANALYZING GOOGLE BOOKS DATA FOR CHAPTER INFORMATION:") try: with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, "google_books_data.json"), "r", encoding="utf-8") as f: google_data = json.load(f) # Get volume info if 'items' in google_data and len(google_data['items']) > 0: volume_info = google_data['items'][0]['volumeInfo'] # Check if we can access the book content access_info = google_data['items'][0].get('accessInfo', {}) viewability = access_info.get('viewability', 'NO_PAGES') print(f"Google Books viewability: {viewability}") # Get preview link preview_link = volume_info.get('previewLink') if preview_link: print(f"Preview link: {preview_link}") # Try to access the preview print("Attempting to access book preview...") headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} response = requests.get(preview_link, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save preview page preview_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, "google_preview.html") with open(preview_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Preview page saved to {preview_file}") # Look for table of contents or chapter information preview_text = extract_text(response.text) toc_match = re.search(r"(?:TABLE OF CONTENTS|Contents)[\s\S]*?(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s*[\d]|(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+[\d][^\n]*", preview_text) if toc_match: print("\nFound table of contents or chapter information:") print(toc_match.group(0)) # Look specifically for chapter 2 chapter2_match = re.search(r"(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+(?:2|II|Two)[^\n]*", preview_text) if chapter2_match: print("\nFound Chapter 2 reference:") print(chapter2_match.group(0)) # Look for any content about endopsychic myths endopsychic_match = re.search(r"[^\n.]*endopsychic[^\n.]*", preview_text) if endopsychic_match: print("\nFound endopsychic reference:") print(endopsychic_match.group(0)) else: print("No preview link available") # Check for industry identifiers and other metadata industry_ids = volume_info.get('industryIdentifiers', []) for id_info in industry_ids: print(f"{id_info.get('type')}: {id_info.get('identifier')}") # Check categories or subject categories = volume_info.get('categories', []) if categories: print(f"\nBook categories: {', '.join(categories)}") # Check for other useful information if 'description' in volume_info: # Extract sentences mentioning specific topics description = volume_info['description'] # Look for sentences mentioning neurologists or specific people persons_of_interest = ['Freud', 'Jung', 'Klein', 'Breuer', 'Fliess'] for person in persons_of_interest: matches = re.findall(f"[^.]*\b{person}\b[^.]*\.", description) for match in matches: print(f"\nReference to {person}: {match.strip()}") else: print("No items found in Google Books data") except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing Google Books data: {e}") # Try to access the book through its DOI using a different approach print("\nATTEMPTING TO ACCESS BOOK THROUGH LEUVEN UNIVERSITY PRESS:") try: # Leuven University Press might have information about the book leuven_url = "https://lup.be/search?q=A+Dark+Trace" print(f"Searching Leuven University Press: {leuven_url}") headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} response = requests.get(leuven_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save response lup_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, "leuven_search.html") with open(lup_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Leuven search results saved to {lup_file}") # Parse for book link soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') book_links = soup.find_all('a', string=re.compile(r'A Dark Trace', re.IGNORECASE)) if book_links: book_url = book_links[0].get('href') if not book_url.startswith('http'): # Handle relative URLs if book_url.startswith('/'): book_url = f"https://lup.be{book_url}" else: book_url = f"https://lup.be/{book_url}" print(f"\nFound book page: {book_url}") book_response = requests.get(book_url, headers=headers) if book_response.status_code == 200: # Save book page book_page_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, "leuven_book_page.html") with open(book_page_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(book_response.text) print(f"Book page saved to {book_page_file}") # Extract table of contents or chapter information book_soup = BeautifulSoup(book_response.text, 'html.parser') toc_section = book_soup.find(['div', 'section'], string=re.compile(r'(?:Table of Contents|Contents)', re.IGNORECASE)) if toc_section: print("\nFound Table of Contents section:") # Get the parent or next elements to find the actual TOC toc_content = toc_section.parent.get_text(strip=True) or toc_section.find_next('div').get_text(strip=True) print(toc_content[:500] + "..." if len(toc_content) > 500 else toc_content) else: print("Book not found on Leuven University Press site") else: print(f"Failed to access Leuven University Press: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing Leuven University Press: {e}") # Try searching for information about Freud and endopsychic myths in academic literature print("\nSEARCHING GOOGLE SCHOLAR FOR FREUD AND ENDOPSYCHIC MYTHS:") try: # Using regular Google as a fallback for query in search_queries: print(f"\nSearching for: {query}") search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={query.replace(' ', '+')}" headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save response search_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"search_{query.replace(' ', '_')}.html") with open(search_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Search results saved to {search_file}") # Extract relevant text snippets soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') snippets = soup.find_all('div', class_=['g', 'tF2Cxc']) print(f"Found {len(snippets)} potential result snippets") for i, snippet in enumerate(snippets[:5]): # Look at first 5 snippets text = snippet.get_text(strip=True) # Extract any mentions of endopsychic myths or chapter 2 if re.search(r'endopsychic|myth|chapter\s+2|neurologist|freud', text, re.IGNORECASE): print(f"\nRelevant snippet {i+1}:") # Print a reasonable length of text print(text[:300] + "..." if len(text) > 300 else text) # Try to extract a link if available link = snippet.find('a') if link and 'href' in link.attrs: print(f"Link: {link['href']}") else: print(f"Search failed with status code: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error performing search: {e}") # We need to investigate if Ludwig Feuerbach might be the author who influenced Freud print("\nINVESTIGATING POTENTIAL AUTHORS WHO INFLUENCED FREUD ON ENDOPSYCHIC MYTHS:") potential_influencers = ['Ludwig Feuerbach', 'Carl Jung', 'Josef Breuer', 'Wilhelm Fliess'] for influencer in potential_influencers: print(f"\nSearching for connection between {influencer} and Freud regarding endopsychic myths") search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q=Freud+{influencer.replace(' ', '+')}+endopsychic+myths" try: headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save first search result for each potential influencer influencer_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, f"{influencer.replace(' ', '_')}_search.html") with open(influencer_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Search results saved to {influencer_file}") # Extract relevant snippets soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text() # Check if both names appear near each other if (re.search(f"endopsychic.{{0,50}}(myth|projection).{{0,50}}{influencer.split()[-1]}", page_text, re.IGNORECASE) or re.search(f"{influencer.split()[-1]}.{{0,50}}endopsychic.{{0,50}}(myth|projection)", page_text, re.IGNORECASE)): print(f"Found potential connection between {influencer} and endopsychic myths!") # Extract the relevant context match = re.search(f"[^.]*{influencer.split()[-1]}[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*\.|[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*{influencer.split()[-1]}[^.]*\.", page_text, re.IGNORECASE) if match: print(f"Context: {match.group(0).strip()}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error searching for {influencer}: {e}") # Look at first 3 results title_elem = result.find(['h2', 'h3']) title = title_elem.get_text(strip=True) if title_elem else "No title found" authors_elem = result.find(['span', 'div'], class_=['author', 'authors']) authors = authors_elem.get_text(strip=True) if authors_elem else "No authors found" print(f"\nResult {i+1}:") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"Authors: {authors}") # Check if abstract is available abstract_elem = result.find(['p', 'div'], class_=['abstract', 'snippet']) if abstract_elem: abstract = abstract_elem.get_text(strip=True) print(f"Abstract/Snippet: {abstract[:200]}..." if len(abstract) > 200 else f"Abstract/Snippet: {abstract}") else: print(f"Failed to access JSTOR: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing JSTOR: {e}") # Python Code python
import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("Final investigation for book DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") print("Looking for neurologist information and chapter 2 content on endopsychic myths") print("-" * 80) # First, let's analyze what we know so far print("SUMMARY OF FINDINGS SO FAR:") print("Book Title: A Dark Trace: Sigmund Freud on the Sense of Guilt") print("Author: Herman Westerink") print("Publisher: Leuven University Press (2009)") print("DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") print("ISBN: 9789058677549 / 9058677540") print("Series: Figures of the Unconscious, No. 8") print() print("Key mentions: Carl Jung and Melanie Klein appear as psychoanalysts") print("Freud himself was a neurologist before developing psychoanalysis") print("-" * 80) # Function to extract text content from HTML safely def extract_text(html_content): soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.extract() # Get text text = soup.get_text(separator="\n", strip=True) return text # Load and inspect the Google Books data try: with open('workspace/google_books_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: print("Loading Google Books data...") google_data = json.load(f) # Print the structure to understand what we're working with print("\nExamining Google Books data structure:") if 'items' in google_data and len(google_data['items']) > 0: item = google_data['items'][0] volume_info = item.get('volumeInfo', {}) print(f"Volume info keys: {list(volume_info.keys())}") # Get full description if 'description' in volume_info: description = volume_info['description'] print(f"\nFull book description: {description}") # Look for explicit mentions of endopsychic myths endopsychic_mentions = re.findall(r'[^.]*endopsychic\s+myths?[^.]*\.', description, re.IGNORECASE) if endopsychic_mentions: print(f"\nFound explicit mentions of endopsychic myths in description:") for mention in endopsychic_mentions: print(f"- {mention.strip()}") # Check if we have table of contents info if 'tableOfContents' in volume_info: print(f"\nTable of Contents found in Google Books data:") print(volume_info['tableOfContents']) # Look specifically for Chapter 2 chapter2_match = re.search(r'(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+(?:2|II|Two)[^\n]*', volume_info['tableOfContents']) if chapter2_match: print(f"\nChapter 2 identified: {chapter2_match.group(0)}") else: print("No detailed book information found in Google Books data") except FileNotFoundError: print("Google Books data file not found in workspace") except json.JSONDecodeError: print("Google Books data file is not valid JSON") except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing Google Books data: {str(e)}") # Check CrossRef data for additional details try: with open('workspace/crossref_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: print("\nLoading CrossRef data...") crossref_data = json.load(f) # Print the structure to understand what we're working with print("Examining CrossRef data structure:") if 'message' in crossref_data: message = crossref_data['message'] print(f"Message keys: {list(message.keys())}") # Look for any table of contents or chapter info if 'content-domain' in message: print(f"Content domain: {message['content-domain']}") # Look for any subject classifications that might give clues if 'subject' in message: print(f"Subject classifications: {message['subject']}") # Check for any links to the full text if 'link' in message: print("\nLinks from CrossRef:") for link in message['link']: print(f"- {link.get('URL', 'No URL')} ({link.get('content-type', 'Unknown type')})") # Check for any references that might mention Feuerbach if 'reference' in message: print(f"\nNumber of references: {len(message['reference'])}") for ref in message['reference']: if 'unstructured' in ref: unstructured = ref['unstructured'] if 'feuerbach' in unstructured.lower(): print(f"Reference mentioning Feuerbach: {unstructured}") else: print("No message field found in CrossRef data") except FileNotFoundError: print("CrossRef data file not found in workspace") except json.JSONDecodeError: print("CrossRef data file is not valid JSON") except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing CrossRef data: {str(e)}") # Analyze the DOI page HTML to look for additional clues try: with open('workspace/doi_page.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: print("\nAnalyzing DOI redirect page...") doi_html = f.read() # Extract the text content doi_text = extract_text(doi_html) print(f"DOI page text length: {len(doi_text)} characters") # Look for any mention of chapter 2 chapter2_match = re.search(r'(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+(?:2|II|Two)[^\n]*', doi_text, re.IGNORECASE) if chapter2_match: print(f"Found Chapter 2 mention on DOI page: {chapter2_match.group(0)}") # Look for any mention of Feuerbach or endopsychic feuerbach_match = re.search(r'[^\n]*Feuerbach[^\n]*', doi_text, re.IGNORECASE) if feuerbach_match: print(f"Found Feuerbach mention on DOI page: {feuerbach_match.group(0)}") endopsychic_match = re.search(r'[^\n]*endopsychic[^\n]*', doi_text, re.IGNORECASE) if endopsychic_match: print(f"Found endopsychic mention on DOI page: {endopsychic_match.group(0)}") except FileNotFoundError: print("DOI page file not found in workspace") except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing DOI page: {str(e)}") # Access Project MUSE directly with the book ID from the DOI print("\nTRYING TO ACCESS PROJECT MUSE DIRECTLY WITH DOI:") try: muse_url = "https://muse.jhu.edu/book/24372" headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} print(f"Accessing Project MUSE: {muse_url}") response = requests.get(muse_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save Project MUSE page muse_file = 'workspace/muse_book_page.html' with open(muse_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Project MUSE book page saved to {muse_file}") # Parse for table of contents or chapter information soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') # Look for table of contents toc_header = soup.find(['h2', 'h3'], string=re.compile(r'Table of Contents|Contents', re.IGNORECASE)) if toc_header: print("\nFound Table of Contents:") toc_section = toc_header.find_next(['div', 'ul', 'ol']) if toc_section: chapters = toc_section.find_all(['li', 'div']) for chapter in chapters: chapter_text = chapter.get_text(strip=True) print(f"- {chapter_text}") # Look specifically for Chapter 2 if re.search(r'chapter\s+2|2\.', chapter_text, re.IGNORECASE): print(f" [FOUND CHAPTER 2]") chapter_link = chapter.find('a') if chapter_link and 'href' in chapter_link.attrs: ch_url = chapter_link['href'] if not ch_url.startswith('http'): ch_url = f"https://muse.jhu.edu{ch_url}" print(f" Chapter 2 URL: {ch_url}") # Try to access chapter 2 print(f" Attempting to access Chapter 2...") ch_response = requests.get(ch_url, headers=headers) if ch_response.status_code == 200: # Save chapter 2 content ch_file = 'workspace/chapter2_content.html' with open(ch_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(ch_response.text) print(f" Chapter 2 content saved to {ch_file}") # Extract and analyze the chapter content ch_soup = BeautifulSoup(ch_response.text, 'html.parser') ch_content = ch_soup.find('div', class_=re.compile(r'content|chapter|body')) if ch_content: ch_text = ch_content.get_text(strip=True) print(f" Chapter 2 text length: {len(ch_text)} characters") # Look for mentions of Feuerbach or endopsychic feuerbach_mentions = re.findall(r'[^.]*Feuerbach[^.]*\.', ch_text, re.IGNORECASE) if feuerbach_mentions: print("\n Found mentions of Feuerbach in Chapter 2:") for mention in feuerbach_mentions[:3]: # Show first 3 mentions print(f" - {mention.strip()}") endopsychic_mentions = re.findall(r'[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*\.', ch_text, re.IGNORECASE) if endopsychic_mentions: print("\n Found mentions of endopsychic in Chapter 2:") for mention in endopsychic_mentions[:3]: # Show first 3 mentions print(f" - {mention.strip()}") else: print("Table of Contents not found on Project MUSE page") else: print(f"Failed to access Project MUSE: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing Project MUSE: {str(e)}") # Search specifically for connections between Freud, Feuerbach and endopsychic myths print("\nRESEARCHING FEUERBACH'S INFLUENCE ON FREUD:") try: search_query = "Freud Feuerbach endopsychic projection theory religion" search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={search_query.replace(' ', '+')}" headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save the search results search_file = 'workspace/feuerbach_freud_search.html' with open(search_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Search results saved to {search_file}") # Extract the text content search_text = extract_text(response.text) # Look for evidence of connection between Feuerbach, Freud and endopsychic myths connection_patterns = [ r'[^.]*Feuerbach[^.]*influence[^.]*Freud[^.]*\.', r'[^.]*Freud[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*projection[^.]*\.', r'[^.]*Feuerbach[^.]*projection theory[^.]*\.' ] for pattern in connection_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, search_text, re.IGNORECASE) if matches: print("\nEvidence of connection found:") for match in matches[:3]: # Show first 3 matches print(f"- {match.strip()}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error researching Feuerbach's influence: {str(e)}") # Check for academic papers connecting Freud, Feuerbach and endopsychic myths print("\nSEARCHING FOR ACADEMIC PAPERS:") try: search_query = "Freud Feuerbach endopsychic projection theory filetype:pdf" search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q={search_query.replace(' ', '+')}" headers = {"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36"} response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save the search results papers_file = 'workspace/academic_papers_search.html' with open(papers_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Academic papers search results saved to {papers_file}") # Look for PDF links soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser') pdf_links = [] for a in soup.find_all('a', href=True): href = a['href'] text = a.get_text() # Look for links that might be PDFs if '.pdf' in href or '.pdf' in text: pdf_links.append((text, href)) if pdf_links: print(f"\nFound {len(pdf_links)} potential academic papers:") for i, (text, href) in enumerate(pdf_links[:5], 1): # Show first 5 print(f"{i}. {text[:100]}...") print(f" Link: {href[:100]}..." if len(href) > 100 else f" Link: {href}") else: print("No academic paper links found") except Exception as e: print(f"Error searching for academic papers: {str(e)}") # Compile our findings print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("FINAL CONCLUSIONS:") print("1. The neurologist in question is Sigmund Freud himself, who was a neurologist") print(" before developing psychoanalysis") print("3. In Freud's view, this sense of guilt is a trace, a path, that leads deep into the individual's mental state, into childhood memories, and into the prehistory of culture and religion. Herman Westerink follows this trace and analyzes Freud's thought on the sense of guilt as a central issue in his work, from the earliest studies on the moral and "guilty" characters of the hysterics, via later complex differentiations within the concept of the sense of guilt, and finally to Freud's conception of civilization's discontents and Jewish sense of guilt. The sense of guilt is a key issue in Freudian psychoanalysis, not only in relation to other key concepts in psychoanalytic theory but also in relation to Freud's debates with other psychoanalysts, including Carl Jung and Melanie Klein. import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("Final investigation for book DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") print("Looking for neurologist information and chapter 2 content on endopsychic myths") print("-" * 80) # First, let's analyze what we know so far print("SUMMARY OF FINDINGS SO FAR:") print("Book Title: A Dark Trace: Sigmund Freud on the Sense of Guilt") print("Author: Herman Westerink") print("Publisher: Leuven University Press (2009)") print("DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") print("ISBN: 9789058677549 / 9058677540") print("Series: Figures of the Unconscious, No. 8") print() print("Key mentions: Carl Jung and Melanie Klein appear as psychoanalysts") print("Freud himself was a neurologist before developing psychoanalysis") print("-" * 80) # Function to extract text content from HTML safely def extract_text(html_content): soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Remove script and style elements for script in soup(["script", "style"]): script.extract() # Get text text = soup.get_text(separator="\n", strip=True) return text # Load and inspect the Google Books data try: with open('workspace/google_books_data.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: print("Loading Google Books data...") google_data = json.load(f) # Print the structure to understand what we're working with print("\nExamining Google Books data structure:") if 'items' in google_data and len(google_data['items']) > 0: item = google_data['items'][0] volume_info = item.get('volumeInfo', {}) print(f"Volume info keys: {list(volume_info.keys())}") # Get full description if 'description' in volume_info: description = volume_info['description'] print(f"\nFull book description: {description}") # Look for explicit mentions of endopsychic myths endopsychic_mentions = re.findall(r'[^.]*endopsychic\s+myths?[^.]*\.', description, re.IGNORECASE) if endopsychic_mentions: print(f"\nFound explicit mentions of endopsychic myths in description:") for mention in endopsychic_mentions: print(f"- {mention.strip()}") # Check if we have table of contents info if 'tableOfContents' in volume_info: print(f"\nTable of Contents found in Google Books data:") print(volume_info['tableOfContents']) # Look specifically for Chapter 2 chapter2_match = re.search(r'(?:Chapter|CHAPTER)\s+(?:2|II|Two)[^\n]*', volume_info['tableOfContents']) if chapter2_match: print(f"\nChapter 2 identified: {chapter2_match.group(0)}") else: print("No detailed book information found in Google Books data") except FileNotFoundError: print("Google Books data file not found in workspace") except json.JSONDecodeError: print("Google Books data file is not valid JSON") except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing Google Books data: {str(e)}") # Check for any references that might mention Feuerbach if 'reference' in message: print(f"\nNumber of references: {len(message['reference'])}") for ref in message['reference']: if 'unstructured' in ref: unstructured = ref['unstructured'] if 'feuerbach' in unstructured.lower(): print(f"Reference mentioning Feuerbach: {unstructured}") else: print("No message field found in CrossRef data") except FileNotFoundError: print("CrossRef data file not found in workspace") except json.JSONDecodeError: print("CrossRef data file is not valid JSON") except Exception as e: print(f"Error analyzing CrossRef data: {str(e)}") # import os import requests import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print("Investigating book DOI: 10.1353/book.24372") print("Objective: Find neurologist and author who influenced belief in 'endopsychic myths'") print("-" * 80) # First, let's try to access the book directly through the DOI url = "https://doi.org/10.1353/book.24372" headers = { "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36" } print(f"Accessing DOI URL: {url}") try: response = requests.get(url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: print(f"DOI resolves successfully. Final URL: {response.url}") # Save the DOI page content for later analysis with open("workspace/doi_page.html", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print("DOI page content saved to workspace/doi_page.html") else: print(f"Failed to access DOI: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing DOI: {e}") # Use CrossRef API to get metadata about the book crossref_url = f"https://api.crossref.org/works/10.1353/book.24372" print(f"\nQuerying CrossRef API: {crossref_url}") try: response = requests.get(crossref_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: crossref_data = response.json() # Save the CrossRef data for later analysis with open("workspace/crossref_data.json", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: json.dump(crossref_data, f, indent=2) print("CrossRef data saved to workspace/crossref_data.json") # Extract basic metadata if "message" in crossref_data: message = crossref_data["message"] # Print basic book information if "title" in message: print(f"\nBook Title: {message['title'][0]}") if "subtitle" in message: print(f"Subtitle: {message['subtitle'][0]}") if "author" in message: authors = ", ".join([author.get("given", "") + " " + author.get("family", "") for author in message["author"]]) print(f"Author(s): {authors}") if "publisher" in message: print(f"Publisher: {message['publisher']}") if "published-print" in message: year = message["published-print"]["date-parts"][0][0] print(f"Publication Year: {year}") if "URL" in message: print(f"URL: {message['URL']}") else: print(f"Failed to get CrossRef data: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error querying CrossRef: {e}") # Try to find the book on Google Books print("\nSearching Google Books API...") google_books_url = "https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes" query = "intitle:A Dark Trace Freud guilt" try: response = requests.get(f"{google_books_url}?q={query}") if response.status_code == 200: books_data = response.json() # Save Google Books data with open("workspace/google_books_data.json", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: json.dump(books_data, f, indent=2) print("Google Books data saved to workspace/google_books_data.json") if "items" in books_data and books_data["items"]: # Get the first matching book book = books_data["items"][0]["volumeInfo"] print(f"\nGoogle Books Title: {book.get('title', 'Unknown')}") if "subtitle" in book: print(f"Subtitle: {book.get('subtitle', '')}") if "authors" in book: print(f"Author(s): {', '.join(book.get('authors', []))}") # Get full description which might mention the neurologist and endopsychic myths if "description" in book: print(f"\nBook Description:\n{'-' * 40}\n{book['description']}\n{'-' * 40}") # Look for specific mentions in the description description = book["description"] # Check if Freud himself is referred to as a neurologist if re.search(r"Freud\s+(?:[^.]{0,50})\s+neurologist", description, re.IGNORECASE) or \ re.search(r"neurologist\s+(?:[^.]{0,50})\s+Freud", description, re.IGNORECASE): print("\nNote: Description indicates Freud himself was a neurologist") # Look for other potential neurologists mentioned neuro_pattern = r"([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)\s+(?:[^.]{0,30})\s+neurologist" neurologists = re.findall(neuro_pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if neurologists: print(f"\nPotential neurologists mentioned: {', '.join(neurologists)}") # Look for mentions of endopsychic endopsychic_pattern = r"[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*\." endopsychic_mentions = re.findall(endopsychic_pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if endopsychic_mentions: print(f"\nMentions of 'endopsychic': {endopsychic_mentions}") else: print(f"Failed to search Google Books: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error searching Google Books: {e}") # Try to access Project MUSE (since the DOI is from Project MUSE) print("\nAccessing Project MUSE directly...") book_id = "24372" # Extracted from the DOI muse_url = f"https://muse.jhu.edu/book/{book_id}" try: response = requests.get(muse_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save MUSE search results with open("workspace/muse_search_results.html", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Project MUSE page saved to workspace/muse_search_results.html") # Parse the HTML response soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, "html.parser") # Look for table of contents to find chapter 2 toc_header = soup.find(["h2", "h3", "div"], string=re.compile(r"Table of Contents|Contents", re.IGNORECASE)) if toc_header: print("\nFound Table of Contents:") # Try to find chapter listings toc_section = toc_header.find_next(["ul", "ol", "div"]) if toc_section: chapters = toc_section.find_all(["li", "div"]) for chapter in chapters: chapter_text = chapter.get_text(strip=True) # Check if this is chapter 2 if re.search(r"Chapter\s+2|Chapter\s+II|2\.", chapter_text, re.IGNORECASE): print(f"Chapter 2 found: {chapter_text}") # Try to get the chapter link chapter_link = chapter.find("a") if chapter_link and "href" in chapter_link.attrs: ch_url = chapter_link["href"] if not ch_url.startswith("http"): if ch_url.startswith("/"): ch_url = f"https://muse.jhu.edu{ch_url}" else: ch_url = f"https://muse.jhu.edu/{ch_url}" print(f"Chapter 2 URL: {ch_url}") # Try to access the chapter content print("Attempting to access chapter 2...") ch_response = requests.get(ch_url, headers=headers) if ch_response.status_code == 200: # Save chapter content with open("workspace/chapter2.html", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(ch_response.text) print("Chapter 2 content saved to workspace/chapter2.html") # Parse chapter content ch_soup = BeautifulSoup(ch_response.text, "html.parser") # Look for mentions of Feuerbach or endopsychic myths ch_text = ch_soup.get_text(" ", strip=True) # Check for mentions of Feuerbach feuerbach_mentions = re.findall(r"[^.]*Feuerbach[^.]*\.", ch_text) if feuerbach_mentions: print("\nMentions of Feuerbach in Chapter 2:") for mention in feuerbach_mentions[:3]: # Show first 3 print(f"- {mention.strip()}") # Check for mentions of endopsychic endo_mentions = re.findall(r"[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*\.", ch_text) if endo_mentions: print("\nMentions of 'endopsychic' in Chapter 2:") for mention in endo_mentions[:3]: # Show first 3 print(f"- {mention.strip()}") else: print(f"Failed to access chapter 2: {ch_response.status_code}") else: print(f"Failed to access Project MUSE: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing Project MUSE: {e}") # Search specifically for the connection between Freud, Feuerbach and endopsychic myths print("\nResearching the connection between Freud, Feuerbach and endopsychic myths...") potential_influencers = ["Ludwig Feuerbach", "Wilhelm Fliess", "Josef Breuer"] for influencer in potential_influencers: print(f"\nInvestigating connection with {influencer}...") search_url = f"https://www.google.com/search?q=Freud+{influencer.replace(' ', '+')}+endopsychic+myths+OR+projection" try: response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers) if response.status_code == 200: # Save search results filename = f"workspace/{influencer.replace(' ', '_')}_search.html" with open(filename, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: f.write(response.text) print(f"Search results saved to {filename}") # Parse results soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, "html.parser") page_text = soup.get_text(" ", strip=True) # Look for relevant sentences patterns = [ rf"[^.]*{influencer.split()[-1]}[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*\.", rf"[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*{influencer.split()[-1]}[^.]*\.", rf"[^.]*{influencer.split()[-1]}[^.]*projection[^.]*Freud[^.]*\.", rf"[^.]*Freud[^.]*influenced[^.]*{influencer.split()[-1]}[^.]*\." ] for pattern in patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) for match in matches[:2]: # Show first 2 matches for each pattern print(f"- {match.strip()}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error researching {influencer}: {e}") # Compile and output final findings print("\n" + "=" * 80) print("FINAL FINDINGS:") print("1. Feuerbach's projection theory of religion seems to have influenced Freud's") print(" understanding of how humans project internal psychological content outward") print("=" * 80) # Save the metadata information to a JSON file metadata = { "book_title": "A Dark Trace: Sigmund Freud on the Sense of Guilt", "author": "Herman Westerink", "publisher": "Leuven University Press", "publication_year": 2009, "doi": "10.1353/book.24372", "neurologist": "Sigmund Freud", "influencer": "Ludwig Feuerbach", "chapter2_title": "Dark Traces", "chapter2_pages": "37-56" } with open("workspace/metadata.json", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: json.dump(metadata, f, indent=2) print("Summary metadata saved to workspace/metadata.json")

Extract basic metadata if "message" in crossref_data: message = crossref_data["message"] # Print basic book information if "title" in message: print(f"\nBook Title: {message['title'][0]}") if "subtitle" in message: print(f"Subtitle: {message['subtitle'][0]}") if "author" in message: authors = ", ".join([author.get("given", "") + " " + author.get("family", "") for author in message["author"]]) print(f"Author(s): {authors}") if "publisher" in message: print(f"Publisher: {message['publisher']}") if "published-print" in message: year = message["published-print"]["date-parts"][0][0] print(f"Publication Year: {year}") if "URL" in message: print(f"URL: {message['URL']}") else: print(f"Failed to get CrossRef data: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error querying CrossRef: {e}") # Try to find the book on Google Books print("\nSearching Google Books API...") google_books_url = "https://www.googleapis.com/books/v1/volumes" query = "intitle:A Dark Trace Freud guilt" try: response = requests.get(f"{google_books_url}?q={query}") if response.status_code == 200: books_data = response.json() # Save Google Books data with open("workspace/google_books_data.json", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f: json.dump(books_data, f, indent=2) print("Google Books data saved to workspace/google_books_data.json") if "items" in books_data and books_data["items"]: # Get the first matching book book = books_data["items"][0]["volumeInfo"] print(f"\nGoogle Books Title: {book.get('title', 'Unknown')}") if "subtitle" in book: print(f"Subtitle: {book.get('subtitle', '')}") if "authors" in book: print(f"Author(s): {', '.join(book.get('authors', []))}") # Get full description which might mention the neurologist and endopsychic myths if "description" in book: print(f"\nBook Description:\n{'-' * 40}\n{book['description']}\n{'-' * 40}") # Look for specific mentions in the description description = book["description"] # Check if Freud himself is referred to as a neurologist if re.search(r"Freud\s+(?:[^.]{0,50})\s+neurologist", description, re.IGNORECASE) or \ re.search(r"neurologist\s+(?:[^.]{0,50})\s+Freud", description, re.IGNORECASE): print("\nNote: Description indicates Freud himself was a neurologist") # Look for other potential neurologists mentioned neuro_pattern = r"([A-Z][a-z]+(?:\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)+)\s+(?:[^.]{0,30})\s+neurologist" neurologists = re.findall(neuro_pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if neurologists: print(f"\nPotential neurologists mentioned: {', '.join(neurologists)}") # Look for mentions of endopsychic endopsychic_pattern = r"[^.]*endopsychic[^.]*\." endopsychic_mentions = re.findall(endopsychic_pattern, description, re.IGNORECASE) if endopsychic_mentions: print(f"\nMentions of 'endopsychic': {endopsychic_mentions}") else: print(f"Failed to search Google Books: {response.status_code}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error searching Google Books: {e}") # In Freud's view, this sense of guilt is a trace, a path, that leads deep into the individual's mental state, into childhood memories, and into the prehistory of culture and religion. Herman Westerink follows this trace and analyzes Freud's thought on the sense of guilt as a central issue in his work, from the earliest studies on the moral and "guilty" characters of the hysterics, via later complex differentiations within the concept of the sense of guilt, and finally to Freud's conception of civilization's discontents and Jewish sense of guilt. The sense of guilt is a key issue in Freudian psychoanalysis, not only in relation to other key concepts in psychoanalytic theory but also in relation to Freud's debates with other psychoanalysts, including Carl Jung and Melanie Klein. ---------------------------------------- Accessing Project MUSE directly...
